  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer365604328" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15382532200142430197"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380383538i/741748._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote> <b> <i> “You own me, Eva. Wherever I am, whatever I’m doing, I belong to you.” </i></b>  </blockquote><br/><b> Entwined With You was everything I could have wanted! I was thrilled with the story, happy with the ending and now am excited for the next books! </b><br/><br/><b> I LOVED IT!!! 5++ STARS! </b><br/><br/>Since this is book #3 in the series, I am not going to talk about the plot at all here. This is not a standalone and should only be read after both <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13572249.Bared_to_You__Crossfire___1_' title='Bared to You (Crossfire, #1) by Sylvia Day' rel='nofollow noopener'>Bared to You</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13596809.Reflected_in_You__Crossfire___2_' title='Reflected in You (Crossfire, #2) by Sylvia Day' rel='nofollow noopener'>Reflected in You</a>.<br/><br/>First you can all rest easy because there is NO RELATIONSHIP CLIFFHAN</span>
  <span id="freeText15382532200142430197" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380383538i/741748._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> <i> “You own me, Eva. Wherever I am, whatever I’m doing, I belong to you.” </i></b>  </blockquote><br><b> Entwined With You was everything I could have wanted! I was thrilled with the story, happy with the ending and now am excited for the next books! </b><br><br><b> I LOVED IT!!! 5++ STARS! </b><br><br>Since this is book #3 in the series, I am not going to talk about the plot at all here. This is not a standalone and should only be read after both <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13572249.Bared_to_You__Crossfire___1_" title="Bared to You (Crossfire, #1) by Sylvia Day" rel="nofollow noopener">Bared to You</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13596809.Reflected_in_You__Crossfire___2_" title="Reflected in You (Crossfire, #2) by Sylvia Day" rel="nofollow noopener">Reflected in You</a>.<br><br>First you can all rest easy because there is NO RELATIONSHIP CLIFFHANGER!!! In fact, of all the three books so far, I’d say this one had the most resolved ending of all. It ended at a point where Gideon and Eva were together and happy. Yes, there were still many unanswered questions for future books (mostly regarding external plot lines and milestones that Gideon and Eva still have to cross) but there was no relationship cliffhanger!<br><br>There was also real no stupidity and no cheating throughout the book. Yes, the characters made mistakes, but they’re only human. I ‘understood’ everything that both Gideon and Eva did throughout the book. I understood why they messed up and I respected them for trying to fix their mistakes.<br><br>There was a lot of smokin’ hot sex (and I mean H.O.T.) but it didn’t overpower the actual work they put into the relationship. I loved that they didn’t use sex as a distraction for working out their issues. They’d always had intense chemistry and sexual attraction but they were also actively focused just as much on working on the rest of their relationship as well which made them functional as a couple both inside and outside of the bedroom.<br><br>I loved that they had this intensely passionate, tumultuous relationship but at the core of it all was always their strong, unwavering love for each other. Everything else was just details.<br><br><i> Entwined With You </i> started off right where book #2 ended throwing us right back in the story. If it has been a while since you’ve read the last book, I would recommend re-reading at least the last chapter of book #2 before starting this just to get yourself back into the details of the story.<br><br><b> In this book, Gideon and Eva’s journey continues as they fight their inner demons and nightmares and work together at maintaining and building a functional relationship filled with intense desire, love and commitment. </b><br><br>One of my most favorite things about Gideon and Eva as a couple is that they TALK!!! They talk through EVERYTHING! They’ve both been broken by their pasts and are dealing with untold amounts of external stress and yet with them, their relationship always came first. I always knew what their top priority was. I could just feel it. And I absolutely freaking LOVED it.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “I look at you, angel, and I want you so badly. I want to be with you, listen to you, talk to you. I want to hear you laugh and hold you when you cry. I want to sit next to you, breathe the same air, share the same life. I want to wake up to you like this every day forever. I want you.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>Gideon Cross is the ultimate tortured, Alpha hero. He’s completely dominant and possessive but at the same time so vulnerable and broken. Truthfully, protective and possessive doesn’t even begin to describe him though. He’s also loyal, understanding, powerful, and passionate. He is just the perfect balance of everything in my eyes. He is Alpha enough to make me swoon but was always logical and rational in his actions. I absolutely loved that he always put Eva first. He was always thinking of her and it was clear in each one of his actions. If it’s possible, I love him even more after reading this book than I did before starting!<br><br>I’ve always really loved Eva too. Deeply scarred by her past and also still hurt by things that had happened in their relationship (despite it being a missunderstanding), she had to work hard to keep being open. Luckily, Gideon helped balance her out. He was always insisting on working things through together. And at the end of the day, they both just wanted to make things work, and were willing to do anything to bring them closer to each other.<br><br>I loved that they went toe to toe on everything. Yes, Gideon was powerful and dominating but Eva was also strong and independent. They didn’t clash, but rather they complimented each other. Their relationship was always balanced and I could never doubted the value they placed on their relationship. You could feel that they were willing to sacrifice anything for each other and never give up. I just loved it. It was heart warming to an extreme.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “Despite everything, we were stronger than we’d ever been.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>And the HEAT!!!! ohhhhh the intensity!! This has got to be one of the hottest books I’ve ever read! Not that it was literally the most graphic but just that their connection intensified every sexual encounter between them. It was scorching!! Sizzling! And, I’m not going to lie, they certainly took things further in the bedroom than they’d ever gone before. There was definitely an “oh my!!” moment for me at one point ;)<br><br>But like I said, I loved that with them it was never all about the sex. I loved watching them genuinely, step-by-step work through their issues. I loved being able to see their progress and to see them grow both as individuals and as a couple.<br><br>The build up of the book’s ending wasn’t as intense as the last one to be sure but that was totally okay with me. Given the context of the story, it didn’t feel right to have something super intense in that moment and I’m glad the author didn’t put some random drama there just for the sake of sensationalizing it. I respect her for staying true to the characters.<br><br>The ending left us in a good place. My heart is happy and I couldn’t have asked for a better place to pause their story while we wait for the rest of the series to be released.<br><br>It has been confirmed that there will be 2 more books in the series after this one. The Crossfire series will now have 5 books.<br><br>I have loved this series from the start and if the next two books are going to continue Gideon and Eva’s story following the same path that these first 3 books have taken and just continue to develop their relationship together without stupidity or excess drama, then I’m all for it!!! <br><br>At first, I thought I would have wanted the “happily ever after” we would have gotten had this been the final book but I can honestly tell you that I did NOT feel that any of the issues were dragged out, or just “put there” for the sake of creating more text. There was no “drama for drama’s sake” and everything that happened both made sense, kept me engaged (or fanning myself) and was believable for the characters.<br><br>Also, given the amount of issues they still have to work through (which I won’t name in order to keep this spoiler-free), I’m honestly very happy that they’re getting more books. I think their story could easily take two more books to tell it in and there are still so many things that I personally WANT to see them work through that we would never have been able to see if the story had wrapped up in just this one book.<br><br>I know some people said that the ending left them “desperately wanting more”, and while I respect their opinion, I just don’t get it to be honest. The story HAD to end somewhere and since we know there will be more books I was completely happy with the ending. Yes, in the issues external to the relationship, there are still unanswered questions but, if there weren’t any, then how would we ever have more books??<br><br>Gideon and Eva were happy and together at the end. For the ending of a mid-series book, I couldn’t have asked for anything better.<br><br><b> Personally, I loved it. Totally loved it. Gideon and Eva continue to be one of my absolute, all time favorite book couples and I can’t wait for more of their story!<br><br>Basically, if you loved the first two books, you should absolutely read this!! </b><br><br>❤<br><br><b> As a final note, I just want to share this with you. It’s a message from the author that I really love and tells me all that I need to know about this series:<br><br><blockquote> <i> “Is it possible for two abuse survivors to have a functional romantic relationship?” – Eva Tramell </i>
</blockquote> <br>“Eva’s question is the core of the Crossfire series. The answer she receives (“<i>Absolutely.</i>”), gives her hope that she can find her way there with Gideon. I hope their journey touches you the way it has me. We all deserve a happily ever after.” (Sylvia Day) </b><br><br>❤<br><br>My casting for Gideon and Eva:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380374913i/729280._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*******************************<br><br><b><u> VIDEO INTERVIEW with SYLVIA DAY</u> by Aestas Book Blog!!! <br><br>I was given the incredible opportunity to interview Sylvia and ask her questions about her inspiration for the CROSSFIRE series and where she sees the series going in the future!! The interview is spoiler-free! <br><br>✦ WATCH HERE: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://aestasbookblog.com/sylviaday/">http://aestasbookblog.com/sylviaday/</a><br><br>*******************************<br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="&quot;That&#39;s All&quot; Ash" class="user" itemprop="url" name="&quot;That&#39;s All&quot; Ash" href="/user/show/5606933-that-s-all-ash">&quot;That&#39;s All&quot; Ash</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer563099665" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6714471811125749186"><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/JimDisgusted.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><b>You see that? That, right there?<br/><br/>That’s me. Well, I’m slightly more feminine looking with a better rack.<br/><br/>But yeah, that look on that face?<br/><br/>I’m wearing the same one. And I <i>just</i> finished this book. <br/><br/>Now, I know what you, “Crossfire” fanatics, are thinking. </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_lsd1q0Kqka1r31q91o1_500.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413676ra/814867.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_lsd1q0Kqka1r31q91o1_500.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b> But, HOLD ON A SEC! Okie dokie?<br/><br/>I’m a huge fan of Miss Sylvia Day, too! Before I read this, I was <i>counting down the days</i> until it was released.<br/><br/>***So remember that.***<br/><br/>Because… </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_inline_mfeamqwwMv1rb9lpe_zps2752e30b.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413676ra/814868.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_inline_mfeamqwwMv1rb9lpe_zps2752e30b.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b> First of all… this series was planned as a trilogy, right? If</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6714471811125749186" style="display:none"><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/JimDisgusted.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413676i/814866.png" alt=" photo JimDisgusted.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>You see that? That, right there?<br><br>That’s me. Well, I’m slightly more feminine looking with a better rack.<br><br>But yeah, that look on that face?<br><br>I’m wearing the same one. And I <i>just</i> finished this book. <br><br>Now, I know what you, “Crossfire” fanatics, are thinking. </b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_lsd1q0Kqka1r31q91o1_500.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413676ra/814867.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lsd1q0Kqka1r31q91o1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> But, HOLD ON A SEC! Okie dokie?<br><br>I’m a huge fan of Miss Sylvia Day, too! Before I read this, I was <i>counting down the days</i> until it was released.<br><br>***So remember that.***<br><br>Because… </b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_inline_mfeamqwwMv1rb9lpe_zps2752e30b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413676ra/814868.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mfeamqwwMv1rb9lpe_zps2752e30b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> First of all… this series was planned as a trilogy, right? If I’ve read the right blog posts and articles, this series was supposed to be a *trilogy*. And then after the second book, good ol’ Day decided to expand it into FIVE books.<br><br>Now, as much as LOVE Gideon… I was excited! I mean, that was like CHRISTMAS hearing news like that. As long as Gideon was in the picture, I would be stoked if she decided to make it a TWENTY-book series. Sign me up!</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_inline_mm6rdqgjSg1qz4rgp.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413676ra/814869.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mm6rdqgjSg1qz4rgp.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>But then I read this book.<br><br>And see, here’s the problem:<br><br>The first two books were made for a 3-book-series. <br><br>And then this one, the THIRD one… was made for a 5-book-series.<br><br>So, basically, what we have is an author adding water to an AMAZING soup, trying to get it to last longer, right? And praying like <i>hell</i> we don’t notice. </b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/office.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413676ra/814870.gif" alt=" photo office.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Well, I noticed. :)<br><br>AND I AIN’T HAPPY.</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/jimdw3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413676ra/814871.gif" alt=" photo jimdw3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>I mean, so much was going ON in this book… but nothing was happening!!!<br><br>Eva was still worrying about the Nathan debacle.</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Who’s <i>dead</i> by the way. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>And she’s kind of entertaining the idea of Brett, her ex-fling who’s now a mega rockstar.<br><br>I mean, come ON, Eva! Seriously. You have Gideon Cross.<br><br>GIDEON CROSS. What’s there to think about? If you know spending time with an ex-boyfriend or <i>whatever</i> is going to piss off the love of your life… then here’s a brain-boggling idea:<br><br>***Don’t spend time with the EX!*** </b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/dd2ee8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413676ra/814872.gif" alt=" photo dd2ee8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> Other than that… this book was okay. </b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_m4tgz7PScp1r00wtg_zps400db104.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413676ra/814873.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m4tgz7PScp1r00wtg_zps400db104.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>And it should have been MORE than okay!</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/7890f6112c0b7925960efaa915a58a56-dropmic3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413676ra/814874.gif" alt=" photo 7890f6112c0b7925960efaa915a58a56-dropmic3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/429926733?book_show_action=true">Oct 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Georgia ♥ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Georgia ♥ " href="/user/show/9138738-georgia">Georgia ♥ </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer429926733" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5581402756252069973"><b>4 We Are All Officially Crossed/Cross' Stars<br/><br/><i>"If souls could be mated with wishes, ours would be inextricably entwined."</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393650i/757892.jpg' width='359' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Gideon and Eva</b>. What more can I say about a couple that defied all odds, fought everyone and anything standing in their way, clawed each other heart out, fixed it up and put it back to together but never returned it? They just kept them and gave their own to the other to hold safe, forever. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393650i/757893.jpg' width='315' height='271' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>A couple that drowned its problems with sex. That couldn't sleep together, afraid of lash</span>
  <span id="freeText5581402756252069973" style="display:none"><b>4 We Are All Officially Crossed/Cross' Stars<br><br><i>"If souls could be mated with wishes, ours would be inextricably entwined."</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393650i/757892.jpg" width="359" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Gideon and Eva</b>. What more can I say about a couple that defied all odds, fought everyone and anything standing in their way, clawed each other heart out, fixed it up and put it back to together but never returned it? They just kept them and gave their own to the other to hold safe, forever. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393650i/757893.jpg" width="315" height="271" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A couple that drowned its problems with sex. That couldn't sleep together, afraid of lashing out in the midst of a nightmare. That has demons screaming in its head every damn hour of a day and a past that haunts and torments their reality and future. That fear still rules their actions. They dared to dream, to hope but they had to make the ultimate sacrifice to have a chance together. And for Eva to feel safe again.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I won’t apologize. I’d do it again.”</i>
</b><br><br>So, they crumbled and almost died in the process.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393650ra/757894.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“You were with me. The whole time. There wasn’t a second that passed when you weren’t on my mind. You own me, Eva. Wherever I am, whatever I’m doing, I belong to you.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393650ra/757895.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Together again, they have to keep a deadly secret, battle their own deep-rooted fear, family, friends, exes, reporters, police.... HELL the whole damn universe for what is rightfully theirs. Love and a happily ever after. Will Gideon manage it out of sheer force of will or Eva's inability to use caution and just plain logic will once again tear them apart?<br><br><b>
  <i>“You’ll never lose me, angel,” he vowed. “Wherever you go, however far, I’ll be right here with you.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380390835i/752789.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This third installment in the seductive and highly erotic <i>Crossfire</i> Series will push your boundaries, drive you crazy, awake all your senses and make you totally mad. You will fall deeper and irrevocably in love with the one and only Gideon Cross and you will pray for this book not to end.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393650ra/757896.gif" width="400" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/620499.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Gideon is once again a sight to behold. Tender and violent, a wild animal, leashed only by the love of a woman. Possessive, arrogant, protective to the extreme and sexy beyond any measure. I couldn't get enough and I swear that every damn time this amazing man opened his deliciously dirty mouth I had a mini-orgasm.<br><br><b>
  <i>““What the hell was I supposed to do, Eva? I didn’t know you existed.” Gideon’s voice deepened, roughened. “If I’d known you were out there, I would’ve hunted you down. I wouldn’t have waited a second to find you. But I didn’t know, and I settled for less. So did you. We both wasted ourselves on the wrong people.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393650ra/757897.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393650ra/757898.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The rest of the book felt to me like a hot mess, straight out of hell. Eva just plain infuriated me. Her reluctance to take a leap of faith, for the man that committed a FREAKING murder for her was really maddening. Second guessing herself, Gideon and their relationship every second page, being insanely jealous BUT going out and talking with her ex and well... (I will give her that ;)) dealing with a horrific situation with her parents, this girl has a lot on its plate.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/594522.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That's right woman!!! Pull your head out of the sand, look what you got right in front you and SCREW THE WORLD!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393650i/757899.jpg" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Don't get to this book looking for answers and resolutions. You will only get more frustrated. Read it as a chapter in Eva &amp; Gideon's story, another hurdle for them to overcome, a sexy and intense read that will arouse and make your heart sing and simultaneously cry.<br><br><b>WE ALL NEED A MAN LIKE GIDEON IN OUR LIFE!!!</b><br><br><i>My dearest and bestest friends, Debra, Joana and Kristalia, thank you once again for an awesome buddy read. It was a pleasure to share Gideon with you. And it was so much fun drooling over hot pics and complaining about Eva!</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393487ra/757594.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And you can enjoy their AWESOMELY HAWT reviews, here:<br>♦<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/458359738" rel="nofollow noopener">Debra's Review</a><br>♦<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/522576651" rel="nofollow noopener">Joana's Review</a><br>♦<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/426206218" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristalia's Review</a><br><br><b> Keeping reading to find out my reaction to the book's delay from hell, Gideon's ownership and how we managed to pull off one hell of a buddy read.</b><br><br><i>Earlier this year or better, late the PREVIOUS year</i><br><br>I was just browsing through my not-yet-released list, when something unexpected caught my eye...<br><br><i>Entwined with You (Crossfire, #3)<br>by Sylvia Day<br><b>Expected publication: June 4th 2013 by Berkley</b></i> <br><br>COME ON!!! SERIOUSLY?? It was delayed EVEN MORE? NOW, it's freaking JUNE!!!<br>YOU GOT TO BE KIDDING ME....<br>I'm actually experiencing a Gideon withdrawal... *sniff*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393650ra/757900.gif" width="500" height="88" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393650ra/757901.gif" width="500" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>But don't despair!!! My wonderful girlfriends, <i>Kristalia, my personal beautiful crystal and Joana the amazing,</i> reminded me that Gideon is always with us!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393650i/757902.png" width="300" height="140" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>I HAVE SOME GOOD NEWS!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393650ra/757903.gif" width="400" height="205" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>An awesome buddy read on 06/08, to share all the Gideon loving....<br><br>You guessed correctly! Me, Debra, Kristalia and Joana, are setting aside our Karina Halle obsession, to delve into Gideon's seductive world!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393650ra/757904.gif" width="400" height="244" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>No pressure to finish, no worries, pure HOT, FUN!<br>And if you want to join, just let us know! :D<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393650i/757905.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Of course we are, Gideon.... Of course we are...</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393650i/757906.png" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/417909753" />
    <a title="Eda**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6285155-eda"><img alt="Eda**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581410351p2/6285155.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/417909753?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eda**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eda**" href="/user/show/6285155-eda">Eda**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer417909753" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17852844693602611072"><br/><b>
  <i>** 1,5-2 "<u>bored-out-of-my-mind</u>" STARS **</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>November 15th 2014</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391758ra/754359.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm enraged right now because I've just wasted a huge amount of highly valued time on this book that I will never be able to take back.<br/><br/>And why did I have to waste my time on rereading a book I didn't even like in the first place?<br/><br/><b>BECAUSE THE AUTHOR PUT 1,5 YEARS BETWEEN BOOK#3 AND BOOK#4!</b><br/><br/>When I realized that I didn't remember <b>ANYTHING</b> about the story, I was left with no choice but to go through the same torture, again, before Book#4 ca</span>
  <span id="freeText17852844693602611072" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>** 1,5-2 "<u>bored-out-of-my-mind</u>" STARS **</i>
</b><br><br><i>November 15th 2014</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391758ra/754359.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm enraged right now because I've just wasted a huge amount of highly valued time on this book that I will never be able to take back.<br><br>And why did I have to waste my time on rereading a book I didn't even like in the first place?<br><br><b>BECAUSE THE AUTHOR PUT 1,5 YEARS BETWEEN BOOK#3 AND BOOK#4!</b><br><br>When I realized that I didn't remember <b>ANYTHING</b> about the story, I was left with no choice but to go through the same torture, again, before Book#4 came out.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416090090ra/11889211.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>What was the result?</i> I'll get to that...<br><br>Firstly, I would like to thank my lovely ladies <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/31339793-jasmine" rel="nofollow noopener">JASMINE</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/16349243-supreet-the-cupcake-queen" rel="nofollow noopener">SUPREET</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7643503-flo-the-coffee-addict" rel="nofollow noopener">FLO</a> for being all kinds of cute and funny throughout our rather painful Buddy Reread! This was the best BR <b>EVER</b> and...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404502371ra/10248524.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Now let's get to the real issue...</i><br><br>This book was a <b>MESS</b>.<br><br>I won't be nice and polite and say <i>"It wasn't as good as one would expect."</i>...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415461027ra/11793210.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was one of the most BORING, most POINTLESS and my God...the EMPTIEST books ever.<br><br>And I'm an Erotica reader. <i>So that says something.</i><br><br><b>
  <u>What was going wrong with this book?</u>
</b><br><br><b>1)</b> NO PLOT WHATSOEVER.<br><br><b>2)</b> THE SAME SEX SCENES OVER AND OVER AGAIN.<br><br>Even the unnecessary but surprising anal scene was eye-roll inducing. *yawn*<br><br><b>3)</b> THE UNBELIEVABLE LEVELS OF STUPIDITY EVA KEEPS SHOWING.<br><br>I seriously hate her.<br><br><b>4)</b> CARY.<br><br>Ugggh. Such an annoying little pain in the a**.<br><br><b>5)</b> BRETT KLINE.<br><br>Pathetic.<br><br><b>6)</b> ALL OF GIDEON'S EX WH*RES.<br><br>Does Gideon have a magic d*ck or something? What's with all this fuss over him?<br><br><b>7)</b> POINTLESS DETAILS ABOUT ALL THE SUPPORTING CHARACTERS.<br><br>Who the hell cares about them? Everyone is reading this damn series for Gideon, dude. Don't kid yourselves.<br><br><b>8)</b> THE SLOOOOOOOW PACE.<br><br>I still can't believe how the hell I stayed awake till the end.<br><br><b>
  <u>What was going right with this book?</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416090090i/11889212.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Not even Gideon Cross. Yes. I'm sorry.<br><br><b>
  <u>Will Eda read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17876893.Captivated_by_You__Crossfire___4_" title="Captivated by You (Crossfire, #4) by Sylvia Day" rel="nofollow noopener">Captivated by You</a>?</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392651735ra/8589773.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Why?</i><br><br>Because I know even now that it will be <b>BAD</b> and I have an itching for a good ol' ranting review. <i>*rubs hands*</i><br><br>Plus, how could I ever pass the chance to BuddyRead with my awesome besties once more?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410538069ra/11120999.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://www.sylviaday.com/captivated-chapters/" rel="nofollow noopener">FIRST THREE CHAPTERS OF "CAPTIVATED BY YOU"</a><br><br>It annoyed the hell outta me, so read it at your own expense...<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17852844693602611072" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer632363201" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2615429201754157737"><b>Now that I've finished my re-read, I can jump into book 4. I love me some Gideon and I'm excited to read some more of him <3 </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/d65128b2-3259-4433-a346-997c3cb0a0b5_zpsc9300ed5.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424053i/845238.jpg' alt=' photo d65128b2-3259-4433-a346-997c3cb0a0b5_zpsc9300ed5.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Rate the book... Not Gideon. Rate the book... Not Gideon. This is easier said than done. The book, a solid 3.5 stars... Gideon- 5+ stars, my rating= <b>4 Stars</b>.<br/><br/>Lets take a look at my Gideon...<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/fccb2592-bd25-43fd-8023-80cccc5c9d1e_zps32e8b6de.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424053i/845239._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo fccb2592-bd25-43fd-8023-80cccc5c9d1e_zps32e8b6de.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <blockquote>Gideon Cross had been designed to fuck a woman right out of her mind.</blockquote>
</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/1364ac87-d41e-46a9-92f9-e6511bb654eb_zps559487cc.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424053i/845240._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo 1364ac87-d41e-46a9-92f9-e6511bb654eb_zps559487cc.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>And his Eva...<br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/2ef1d91c-707b-49ca-997f-a755094b4dcf_zpsa42be4b2.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424053i/845241._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 2ef1d91c-707b-49ca-997f-a755094b4dcf_zpsa42be4b2.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <blockquote>We were two halves of the same soul.</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>If you haven’t read <i>Bared to You</i> or <i>Reflect</i></span>
  <span id="freeText2615429201754157737" style="display:none"><b>Now that I've finished my re-read, I can jump into book 4. I love me some Gideon and I'm excited to read some more of him &lt;3 </b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/d65128b2-3259-4433-a346-997c3cb0a0b5_zpsc9300ed5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424053i/845238.jpg" alt=" photo d65128b2-3259-4433-a346-997c3cb0a0b5_zpsc9300ed5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Rate the book... Not Gideon. Rate the book... Not Gideon. This is easier said than done. The book, a solid 3.5 stars... Gideon- 5+ stars, my rating= <b>4 Stars</b>.<br><br>Lets take a look at my Gideon...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/fccb2592-bd25-43fd-8023-80cccc5c9d1e_zps32e8b6de.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424053i/845239._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo fccb2592-bd25-43fd-8023-80cccc5c9d1e_zps32e8b6de.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>Gideon Cross had been designed to fuck a woman right out of her mind.</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/1364ac87-d41e-46a9-92f9-e6511bb654eb_zps559487cc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424053i/845240._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 1364ac87-d41e-46a9-92f9-e6511bb654eb_zps559487cc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And his Eva...<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/2ef1d91c-707b-49ca-997f-a755094b4dcf_zpsa42be4b2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424053i/845241._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 2ef1d91c-707b-49ca-997f-a755094b4dcf_zpsa42be4b2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>We were two halves of the same soul.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>If you haven’t read <i>Bared to You</i> or <i>Reflected in You</i>, you should probably go do that asap, Gideon Cross is not someone you want to miss out on. Also, if you haven’t read the first 2, this review will contain some storyline spoilers so there ya go. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/3f56b7f2-68bc-4a3f-9579-429c38397c6f_zps5f127063.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424053i/845242.jpg" alt=" photo 3f56b7f2-68bc-4a3f-9579-429c38397c6f_zps5f127063.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Entwined with You</i> starts off right where <i>Reflected in You</i> left off. Eva and Gideon are ‘together’ but not publicly. Its not safe for them to be together right now. Gideon has proven time and time again he will go to any extremes necessary to protect Eva. She is willing to do the same for him. Even if it means distancing herself for the time being. The first half of the book was a little repetitive (my main reason for the storyline being only a 3.5-4 rating) a lot of reassurance back and forth, over and over. But hot damn it was HOT! <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Thank you.”<br>“What are you thanking me for? You did all the work.”<br>“There’s no work involved in fucking you, angel.” His slow smile was pure satiated male. “I’m grateful for the privilege.”<br>I sank back onto my heels. “You’re killing me. You can’t be that gorgeous and sexy and say stuff like that. It’s overload. It fries my brain. Sends me into a meltdown.”<br>His smile widened and he kissed me again. “I know the feeling.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br>Eva and Gideon together... yep, panties just melted right off of me. That club scene??? Wow. <br>Gideon wants to make sure Eva knows how much she means to him. He only wants her, no matter what his past was, his life truly began when he met his angel. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/e1cfb330-df05-41b0-82a3-0715ad4392ea_zpsdfb2933c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424053i/845243.jpg" alt=" photo e1cfb330-df05-41b0-82a3-0715ad4392ea_zpsdfb2933c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The second half of the book was much better for me. I was ecstatic that Eva and Gideon were able to get their relationship out in the open again. Not only is Gideon sexy as hell, he gets extra swoony in this book!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/9efa0c27-1013-43bc-a8ac-1ddf59111b80_zps23bc9c85.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424053i/845244._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 9efa0c27-1013-43bc-a8ac-1ddf59111b80_zps23bc9c85.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Towards the end, there is some definite drama and complications. Thankfully, the couple is able to stay strong, united, together. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Whatever we face, we face together. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[And you’ll do it with my name. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>For those of you worried about another <b>dreaded cliffhanger</b>, fear not. I can safely say there is <b>
  <u>NO CLIFFHANGER</u>
</b>. There are some unanswered questions, and some big things that are going to happen in the next book, you can tell, but Eva and Gideon are on solid ground so no worries there ;D I just love Gideon and Eva together. I love that they are two damaged people with broken pasts, but they are perfectly functional together. They really are great for one another. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/efe52412-a62d-4b26-a90f-aa2f5af88c32_zpsf80839c4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424053i/845245.jpg" alt=" photo efe52412-a62d-4b26-a90f-aa2f5af88c32_zpsf80839c4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>At first, I was a little nervous about this series turning into a 5 book series, but seeing how this one ended, I could see how the author would want another book or two to tie up all the loose ends. Eva and Gideon’s story is far from over, and I’m excited to see what is next to come for them! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I was SO FREAKING HAPPY they got married, but I’m looking forward to their actual wedding. I also want to see what happens with the alleged sex tape, Eva’s parent’s indiscretion, and Cary possibly becoming a father... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>On a side note, I’m just going to say how much I LOVE Cary! Yep- love him and his manwhore ways...<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Ever worry about shouting out the wrong name when you’re coming?”<br>“Nope. I just call ‘em all baby.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br>Gideon is one of the hottest alpha’s around, so even if you don’t love the book, you gotta love him!!! And heres to hoping the next book won’t take forever to come out! Happy reading! </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14062541250788700120"><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1362526983l/15731779.jpg' width='300' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>If souls could be mated with wishes, ours would be inextricably entwined.</i>
</b><br/><br/>The third book in the <i>Crossfire</i> series, <b>
  <i>Entwined with You</i>
</b> continues the often tumultuous relationship between Gideon Cross, the twenty-eight year-old billionaire and one of the top twenty-five richest people in the world, and Eva Tramell.<br/><br/>Ms Day does have a lovely writing style, if a little lavender for my tastes in contemporary romance. <br/><br/><i>We'd mistaken our ferocious mutual captivation for lust until we realized we co</i></span>
  <span id="freeText14062541250788700120" style="display:none"><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1362526983l/15731779.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>If souls could be mated with wishes, ours would be inextricably entwined.</i>
</b><br><br>The third book in the <i>Crossfire</i> series, <b>
  <i>Entwined with You</i>
</b> continues the often tumultuous relationship between Gideon Cross, the twenty-eight year-old billionaire and one of the top twenty-five richest people in the world, and Eva Tramell.<br><br>Ms Day does have a lovely writing style, if a little lavender for my tastes in contemporary romance. <br><br><i>We'd mistaken our ferocious mutual captivation for lust until we realized we couldn't breathe without each other.</i><br><br><b>The Plot</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The plot continues some threads from the previous two books. The police investigation into the murder of Eva's stepbrother may not be quite over, although Gideon remains in the clear. Some problems arise for Eva with her past involvement with Brett Kline. Cary, Eva's best friend, has both a steady boyfriend and a steady girlfriend. Some interesting developments there. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>The Relationship</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Still obsessive, still co-dependent, but maturing as well. Gideon presents Eva with a lovely gift towards the end. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Love Scenes</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The love scenes are well-written. Plentiful, but that's to be expected in an erotic CR. Gideon and Eva take their intimacy up a notch with reciprocal anal digital sex. I do have to wonder though why Eva seems to continually press Gideon into this, given his past abuse and his present reluctance.<br><br>We also find out some interesting facts about Gideon's grooming habits! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Is it worth $9.99?</b><br>In my opinion, no. Wait for a library copy.<br><br><b>Is it worth reading?</b><br>Yes, but only if you're a diehard Gideon and Eva fan. <br>If you're sorta interested, just wait for the library copy. Imo, not a great deal happens.<br><br><b>Final Thoughts</b><br>Overall, an average read with a few highlights. Certainly fans of the <i>Crossfire</i> series won't want to miss this. But, if you want to read it, and are reluctant to pay for it, I suggest wait for a library copy. <br><br><b>Steam:</b> 4<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_503790578" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/503790578" />
    <a title="Purva" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14702224-purva"><img alt="Purva" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415818100p2/14702224.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/503790578?book_show_action=true">Jan 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Purva" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Purva" href="/user/show/14702224-purva">Purva</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer503790578" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3739183337916921531"><a href='http://imgur.com/5lcTtBs' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404764ra/787914.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Let me start by saying I loved the first 2 books of this series tremendously. I was besotted with Gideon so i chose to overlook the trivial things about both the books that irked me.<br/><br/>Even this time i've been fairly generous. I've given 3 stars only because i'm blinded by my lust for Gideon.<br/><br/>Why Sylvia Day?<br/>The storyline was already thin and now she's stretching it out hopelessly. She's adding silly plotlines to set the scene for the next 2 books, which i doubt many people will buy.<br/>She's butcher</span>
  <span id="freeText3739183337916921531" style="display:none"><a href="http://imgur.com/5lcTtBs" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404764ra/787914.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Let me start by saying I loved the first 2 books of this series tremendously. I was besotted with Gideon so i chose to overlook the trivial things about both the books that irked me.<br><br>Even this time i've been fairly generous. I've given 3 stars only because i'm blinded by my lust for Gideon.<br><br>Why Sylvia Day?<br>The storyline was already thin and now she's stretching it out hopelessly. She's adding silly plotlines to set the scene for the next 2 books, which i doubt many people will buy.<br>She's butchered up pretty much every character in this book except Gideon. Finishing this book was such a pain.<br><br><b>Eva</b><br><br>She's hypocritical, selfish and immature. Gideon loves her unconditionally, for Christ's sake he killed a man to protect her. I was gritting my teeth whenever Brett appeared in this book. And why she can't say no and straighten out the mess with Brett. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Also why is she grinding against random men in clubs. Her mother gets on my nerves too and in this book she cheated on her husband with Eva's father. Lovely.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/wamkVHy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404764ra/787915.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/C3cqg5F" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404764ra/787916.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Gideon needs to sort out his issues too. Cary is also not likeable and he didn't have much to do in this book. Also i have no interest in the details of Eva's co-workers life, it was needless and boring.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/fjovu0I" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404764ra/787917.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Why is the writer hell bent on describing the way Eva, Gideon, Cary and every freaking character is dressed and their physical attributes in every goddamn scene? Also we don't want to know what they're eating for every meal and which brand they're obsessed with. This has grated me since the first book but i'm less forgiving now.<br>It kills me to say this but this book was just horrible and i'm done with Sylvia Day and the series.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/67oVLH4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404764ra/787918.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10982670314074106489">ETA: JUNE?! Come on guys, you've now missed THREE major selling holidays -Christmas, Valentine's Day and Mother's Day for crying out loud, MOTHER'S DAY WOULD BE A GREAT SELLING POINT FOR THIS SERIES. *Shaking my head baffled* I mean they could've done a trilogy box-set and everything (although I think this series is now going to dragged out longer, now).   <span id="freeText10982670314074106489" style="display:none">ETA: JUNE?! Come on guys, you've now missed THREE major selling holidays -Christmas, Valentine's Day and Mother's Day for crying out loud, MOTHER'S DAY WOULD BE A GREAT SELLING POINT FOR THIS SERIES. *Shaking my head baffled* I mean they could've done a trilogy box-set and everything (although I think this series is now going to dragged out longer, now). Ok that's the end of my rant :).<br /><br />I can understand the publisher's intentions with pushing the release date back- you want to build up the anticipation. However, 5 months is NOT the right decision. I personally think that this is a HUGE mistake on Penguin's part. A large portion of 50 Shades' success relied heavily on the fact that ALL THREE BOOKS WERE AVAILABLE WITHIN A MONTH OF EACH OTHER. <br /><br />I know I will be dealing with a lot of ticked off customers once they realize they won't be able to read the third book until next Spring (my sister included). <br /><br />Christmas is a huge selling season, and this title would have been the perfect gift for wives, daughters, sisters (hell even some men read this series).Penguin will lose readers over this choice, it's unfortunate but true.</span>

</a><br>Best experienced, <b>The Crossfire series is Gideon’s and Eva’s epic love story</b>, both broken, flawed and co-dependent and yet so determined and relentless for their elusive happily-ever after. Follow them through sky-high ups and rock-bottom lows as their relationship is tested with demons from their pasts, envy, jealousy, secrets and lies. Yet their biggest obstacles will always come from within. <b>It’s their journey of self-discovery and fulfillment and about pushing all limits and surrendering it all for love.</b><br><br><u>Books in the Crossfire series must be read in order:</u><br><b>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484192546" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Bared to You</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/495808055" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Reflected in You</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/633237711" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Entwined with You</a><br>Book 4: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/609616039" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Captivated by You</a><br>Book 5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1058838030" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">One with You</a></b><br><br>For me the <b>theme song for Gideon’s and Eva’s story</b> is: <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=R3NVDmzRYnA" rel="nofollow noopener">♫ Listen to Otis Redding’s soulful rendition of “My precious love” ♫</a>. The lyrics <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫<br><i>“Your precious love means more to me than any love<br>Than any love could ever be<br>For when I wanted you I was so lonely and so blue<br>That’s what love, that’s what love really made me do<br><br><b>They keep saying that our love won’t grow now<br>But honey I wanna tell them and I just want to show them<br>How in the world do they know that?</b><br><br>It won’t be long<br>For as long as you’re in love with me<br>I know our love will grow wider <br>And so deeper than any, any ever seen<br><br>Of all the things that I want now<br>In this whole wide world<br>Is just for you to say, for you to say that you’ll be my girl. <br><br><b>And I’m calling, I’m wanting you<br>I just keep wanting you<br>I’m wanting you now<br>Nobody but you now<br>Nobody but you now</b><br><br>Oh I wanna tell you just one more time<br>For your precious love<br>It means everything in the world to me<br>Everything in the world to me<br>And I’m just so wild now<br>Just to have you right home with me.”</i><br>~Otis Redding<br>♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <b> so simply depicts the intensity of Gideon’s love and need for his Eva.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/DayCrossfire1-3HerobySueBee_zpsacdc20a7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401846i/780457.jpg" alt=" photo DayCrossfire1-3HerobySueBee_zpsacdc20a7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Gideon Cross</b> is my ultimate hero. His <b>combination of</b> larger-than life personality and uncanny good looks; enigmatic and elusive; intense and in-control; broken and flawed; ruthless and unyielding, yet when it came to his Eva vulnerable, relentless and human. <br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Honestly, Gideon Cross had been designed to fuck a woman right out of her mind.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>Six words to describe Gideon: <b>Unforgettable, intense, ruthless, enigmatic, dominant and captivating.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/DayCrossfire1-3HeroinebySueBee_zps35566c7e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401846i/780458.jpg" alt=" photo DayCrossfire1-3HeroinebySueBee_zps35566c7e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Like it or not, but <b>Eva Tramell</b> is everything Gideon needed. Five words to describe Eva: <b>Endearing, needy, tenacious, smart and fragile.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Reminds me of the red dress you wore the first time I had you. That was it for me, you know. You devastated me. There was no coming back from that.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>Entwined with you (book 3)</b>, just like book 1 and 2, is very much a rollercoaster; Suspensefully told it’s filled with villains, surprises and shockers, but also beautifully depicting an against-all-odds love and of course in true Sylvia Day fashion plenty of sinfully steamy sex scenes. I like the direction she took in book 3. Ms. Day is a master at spinning a story and she has succeeded with artfully tying in events from previous books without making it feel like a synopsis. Though it did not end with the cliff-hanger of all cliff-hangers it had an abrupt ending. But had I known beforehand I would still have read it! And considering everything that has happened it makes sense to have another two books to wrap it all up.<br><br><b>Epic! Spellbinding! Captivating! Addictive! Unforgettable!</b> In my humble opinion likely to become one of the best love stories of all times! <br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Gideon was a man who’d lived an entirely solitary life, and yet he’d accepted me into it so completely that he could envision a future I was afraid to imagine. I was so scared I’d only be setting myself up for a heartbreak I couldn’t survive.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5+++ stars <br>Heroine rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 5+ stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 5 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: N/A<br>*******************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 5+ stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this series: Yes.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15355942042931708957">3 stars - SPOILERS AHEAD - read a your own risk - am about to be a little ranty too so sorry in advance. <br/>Let me break this one down for you... Gideon & Eva reconnect... talk through their shit.... have glossy & polished porn sex... that's the first 10%. Gideon and Eva continue to reconnect... talk some more... and have some more glossy & polished porn style sex. That takes you up to 20%. OH - then - they talk even more... have some more sex (nicely air brushed - porn style) - and you guessed it.</span>
  <span id="freeText15355942042931708957" style="display:none">3 stars - SPOILERS AHEAD - read a your own risk - am about to be a little ranty too so sorry in advance. <br />Let me break this one down for you... Gideon &amp; Eva reconnect... talk through their shit.... have glossy &amp; polished porn sex... that's the first 10%. Gideon and Eva continue to reconnect... talk some more... and have some more glossy &amp; polished porn style sex. That takes you up to 20%. OH - then - they talk even more... have some more sex (nicely air brushed - porn style) - and you guessed it... takes you up to 30%. Yeah - I got really bored with their 'reconnection'. (Yawn!!) <br />By this time I'm texting one of my BFF's who is also reading at the same time going WTF?! where is the story.... so we start making up some exciting possibilities (none which happen mind you!)<br />so then.... more sex - talking - the percentage continues to climb...<br />There is some minor interference with the other characters which go no where and add no substance to the non-existent storyline... Brett...meh... Corrine... meh. The reporter...burrr - who cares?!<br /><br />They revisit some of the issues and problems from the other books... but nothing really worrying.<br />There was no real crazy drama. No shocks. Oh and I wasn't surprised by what they did on the island too. Saw that coming a mile away... (will keep that part a secret)<br /><br />Then they talk / run into / deal with some sub-characters again when they get back... <br />Yada Yada Yada. But nothing really challenges their relationship or cause any really epic Eva &amp; Gideon explosions...which I was desperately holding out for! and then it just ends. Fin. See ya next time peeps... <br /><br />I mean where was the storyline. I mean WTF! W. T. F. !!! Kindle was tossed across the room! Sent angry texts to my friends venting my frustration and disappointment! and then I yelled a little!<br />Sigh... I feel better now! thanks! :-)<br /><br />So, now you're probably asking yourself... gee, Angela really wasn't impressed by good ol Entwined With You... so why the decent 3 star rating? Ah well I'm happy you asked that question my GR's friends - my reason is three fold,<br />1) even though there was minimal story, the sex they had that filled the majority of the book was really well written. Even though I got bored with it in-between all the love talk, it was still very well written. star 1<br />2) Cary... I like Cary. star 2<br />3) There is ONE EPIC FUCKING AWESOME SEX SCENE that was fan-fucking-tastic. It was around 38/39% in the club (wink wink) those of you who have read it know what I'm talking about. It felt raw, gritty, animalistic and explosive. Everything Gideon &amp; Eva should be! Seriously if book had scenes like the club one all through out my rating would have been much higher, even without a storyline! That one scene - felt to me - everything that I envision Gideon &amp; Eva to be about. BIG STAR number 3!!! seriously love that club scene! Why wasn't that same intensity more present through the rest of the book!??? why god - why!!!!?????<br /><br />so there you go...<br />3 stars ***</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15109093161272724978">I surprised myself....that I actually finished reading this!!!   <span id="freeText15109093161272724978" style="display:none">I surprised myself....that I actually finished reading this!!! At the end....I was totally comatose!!!<br><br>Entwined with You, the 3rd book in Sylvia Day's Crossfire Series was a beyond a total NO NO and more than beyond TEDIOUS!!! Just when I hoped that I could at last "bond" with Gideon Cross.....instead I came out not bonding in any way or form. His only redeeming quality here was how he protected and actually loved Eva and how far he would go to keep her safe. However, I felt that he needs to sort out his bloody issues.<br><br>I began to dislike Eva Tramell to n end. What a selfish, self-centered, two-faced false person....and how hypocritical she was when it came to Gideon. The guy bares his soul to her, kills for her....and she's suddenly unsure about her feelings towards her ex...the douchy Brett....and all the sexy dancing with strange men in clubs...........Gideon, get rid of Eva please!!!!<br><br>Nothing happens in this story....oh, yes....sex and more boring sex happens and nothing else!!! It's one long repeat and repeat and repeat...<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1476498528ra/20849261.gif" alt=" photo 200w_zpssacl2bi9.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>And I must include repetitive comments about the characters sexy bodies, the food they eat, the clothes they wear..blah blah blah........and all those pages and pages of Eva's workmates.......I am soooooooooooooo bored with her boss and his fiancée!!!!     <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1476498529ra/20849262.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mzvmmfGp2K1sjay31o1_500_zpsfmk7bsq7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>OMG....let me not forget.........all those ANGEL's from Gideon!!!!!<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1476498529i/20849263.gif" alt=" photo 200_s_zpsg2eghpow.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>If I read any more ANGEL's, I would have vomited............seriously!!!<blockquote>

  <b>”Honestly, Gideon Cross had been designed to fuck a woman right out of her mind.” <br>You f&amp;cking own me , Eva. I’ll be damned if I don’t own you back <br>"I look at you, angel, and I want you so badly. I want to be with you, listen to you, talk to you. I want to hear you laugh and hold you when you cry.         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer503976439" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1001641469744331545"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404793i/788045._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404793i/788046._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Absolutely blown away! I love these books so much! Just fantastic.<br/><br/>And every time I read another one I fall a little bit more in love with Gideon Cross. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404793i/788047._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But oh my God, the heartache. Jeeez, can't these two catch a break? There could not <i>be</i> more obstacles in their way. My goodness!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"If souls could be mated with wishes, ours would be inextricably entwined."<br/></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I don't even really know what to write right now. I feel like just writing a review that goes something like...<br/><br/>IT'S AMAZING <br/>IT'S AMAZ</span>
  <span id="freeText1001641469744331545" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404793i/788045._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404793i/788046._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Absolutely blown away! I love these books so much! Just fantastic.<br><br>And every time I read another one I fall a little bit more in love with Gideon Cross. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404793i/788047._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But oh my God, the heartache. Jeeez, can't these two catch a break? There could not <i>be</i> more obstacles in their way. My goodness!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"If souls could be mated with wishes, ours would be inextricably entwined."<br></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I don't even really know what to write right now. I feel like just writing a review that goes something like...<br><br>IT'S AMAZING <br>IT'S AMAZING <br>IT'S AMAZING <br>IT'S AMAZING <br>IT'S AMAZING <br>IT'S AMAZING <br><br>... But that would be pretty dull.<br><br>So, I'm going to go with this... If you've already read these books, I'm going to assume I don't need to do a whole lotta selling right now. If you're on book #3, you must be feeling it and you'll know how fantastic and intricate this story has become. So let's do a sales job on those of you who either haven't read them, or read book #1 and left it there...<br><br>READ THE SERIES! Honestly, I promise you, you will not regret it. I will readily admit that when I read the first book, I was like, 'Seriously? 50 Shades mark 2 or what?!'... I mean, sexy billionaire meets innocent young girl, troubled pasts, expensive cars, extravagant gestures. Even the initials were the same... Christian Grey = CG, Gideon Cross = GC. I was thinking 'Does this author have <i>no</i> imagination' ?!?! <br><br><i>But</i>, Gideon fans, refrain from throwing rocks at me because OH MY CHRIST! YES YES YES, Sylvia Day has an <i>amaaaazing</i> imagination. Turns out, she is actually somewhat of a genius! There are more twists and turns and heartache and complication and angst in this story than any other. And it's utterly brilliant. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I'd wait forever for you, as long as you're mine."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I love the writing. I love the characters. I love the dialogue between Gideon and Eva. Oh, it's soooo cute. He says the cutest, but most heartfelt things and it just works soooo well. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Has that line ever worked for anyone?"<br>"I'm not feeding you lines. I mean every word."<br>...<br>"Day One of my life was the day I met you."<br>"Okay, that's a winner. You can put it in."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Really, this is a review, not only of this book, but of the series as a whole, as I read books #1 and #2 before I began blogging and reviewing. And I urge all of you who have not gotten hold of these yet, or who did not give them enough of a chance, to dive in. <br><br>And I am totally stoked that there are two more books in this series now. A friend of mine, who hadn't read <i>Entwined with You</i> yet said 'Oh God, two more books? No! I wanted this to be the last one.'<br>She finished <i>EwY</i> last night and rung me to say 'Oh myyyy Goooooodddd, I can't wait for the second book!!! I never want it to end!' And yes, the words 'I told you so' <i>did</i> leave my lips!<br><br>So, that's it. It's fantastic, it's gripping, it's original, it's sexy and it's absolutely going on my favourites, ✰✰✰✰✰+, need-it-in-paperback shelf!<br>Get some Gideon in your life!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Waking up to you is like... presents on Christmas morning."<br>His mouth curved. "For your convenience, I'm already unwrapped. Batteries not required."<br></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404793i/788048._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389732785i/8051738._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389732785i/8051739._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389732785i/8051740._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389732785i/8051741._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389732785i/8051742._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389732785i/8051743._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>Entwined with You</i> Statistics</b><br><b>Steam Rating (out of 5):</b> ♥♥♥♥♥<br><b>Ending:</b> Cliffhanger<br><b>Series:</b> ✓ <br><b>Reading Order:</b> <br>Book #1 - Bared to You<br>Book #2 - Reflected in You<br>Book #3 - Entwined with You<br>Book #4 - TBC<br>Book #5 - TBC<br><b>Can this be read as a standalone?</b> No<br><b>Themes:</b><br>Billionaire hero<br>Erotica<br><b>Warning. This book includes...</b> Memories of child abuse/rape<br><b>Writing:</b> Amazeballs!<br><br><b>AMAZON UK:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Entwined-You-Crossfire-Novel-ebook/dp/B0090KZDSK/ref=sr_1_2?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1370628093&amp;sr=8-2&amp;keywords=entwined+with+you">http://www.amazon.co.uk/Entwined-You-...</a><br><b>AMAZON US:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Entwined-You-Crossfire-Novel-ebook/dp/B0090KZDSK/ref=sr_1_2?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1370628093&amp;sr=8-2&amp;keywords=entwined+with+you">http://www.amazon.com/Entwined-You-Cr...</a><br><br><b>
