<div id="review_365809578" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/365809578" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/365809578?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101604922" href="/book/show/16078411-entwined-with-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer365809578" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15656445693639547821">In the last book, <i>Reflected in You</i>, Eva found out Gideon's secret and why he had been acting the way he did. Now, they begin working through things and seeing if they are able to move forward with their relationship. <br/><br/>This is the third book in the trilogy that is no longer a trilogy. That being said, it <b>is</b> a middle book. If you go into this thinking anything else, you <i>will</i> be disappointed. It <i>is</i> much slower than the prior books. Things have been sorted out for the moment and it's almost as if it'</span>
  <span id="freeText15656445693639547821" style="display:none">In the last book, <i>Reflected in You</i>, Eva found out Gideon's secret and why he had been acting the way he did. Now, they begin working through things and seeing if they are able to move forward with their relationship. <br><br>This is the third book in the trilogy that is no longer a trilogy. That being said, it <b>is</b> a middle book. If you go into this thinking anything else, you <i>will</i> be disappointed. It <i>is</i> much slower than the prior books. Things have been sorted out for the moment and it's almost as if it's the calm before the storm...you can almost feel that the sh*t is going to hit the fan. <br><br>But we do get a lot of good steamy scenes from Gideon and Eva, after all, they have a lot of making up to do. Unfortunately, they both still have a lot of problems <b>but</b>...I do feel that they are making some progress and they are trusting each other which is a big relief. <br><br>Gideon still keeps things from Eva and it drives me crazy!! And yes, he still has a ton of issues but his focus is very direct. However, I was happy with the ways he tried to make up for the past but he still has a way to go. <br><br><b>
  <u>My Gideon</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379792420i/563316._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Eva has really grown. She realizes how much Gideon wants and needs her and she has decided she does trust him. But...she still does things to push his buttons with other guys including Brett...that I just didn't understand! <br><br>As I mentioned, of course, there are hot, steamy scenes...I mean we are talking about Gideon and Eva after all! ;) I do have to admit while I enjoyed them...the club, the plane, the weekend...my favorite parts were when they were just together, talking and cuddling. Finally! Some time to just "be together" without all that other crap. I can see how people would think it was boring but I just felt it was sooo necessary. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379792420i/563315._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That doesn't mean there weren't problems but for once, the focus on Gideon and Eva wasn't the main problem all the time. Cary's problems keep piling on and he's gotten himself into a "situation"...I'm not sure I really believe it though. Eva's Mom and Dad get themselves in a bit of a fix...and that was kind of weird!! Not really sure where SD is going with that one. Corrine continues to be a major thorn in both Gideon and Eva's side but this time she's pulled out all the strings...and what's going on with her husband, Jean-Francois? Gideon's Mom is being a major b*tch and Brett can't keep his hands off Eva! I don't know why I'm shocked about the video and then the tape! And who was the red-headed woman at the charity event? I also don't trust Deanna the reporter at all!<br><br>There's even more things going on with other characters. At Eva's work, Mark and Steven have some good news, we get to know Will better and Megumi, who's having her own guy troubles. And there's more interaction from the families, Christopher makes an appearance and causes problems naturally. Stanton's nephew, Martin, is getting to know Eva's friend, Lacey, and Ireland's been around more. <br><br>And unfortunately, the problem with Nathan hasn't gone away. Obviously, there is more to the story...and it seems as though it may be a huge factor even though I have no idea how! The situation with the bracelet is driving me crazy!! <br><br>My favorite part was Gideon and Eva's weekend!! I was actually surprised that things went through but I loved how Gideon always takes care of everything and <i>thinks of everything!</i> I especially love how affected he is by certain things that Eva does and says. ~sigh~ <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379792420i/563317.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then the story just kind of ends, right in the middle of things. Eva and Cary are set to go to San Diego for the weekend where Brett will be and Gideon's not happy about it, Corrine's not out of the woods, it's unknown if the situation with Brett and the tape have been handled, and what happened to Megumi?? <br><br>There's a lot to be covered in the next two books and I can't wait!!<br><br>(**Note...if you want more information on what's going on with the books, here's info from SD's facebook page...<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/AuthorSylviaDay/posts/10151469795943457">https://www.facebook.com/AuthorSylvia...</a>)<br><br><br>Favorite quotes:<br><br>♥ “It’s killing me,” he said gruffly. “Being without you. Missing you. I feel like my f*cking sanity depends on you, Eva, and you want me to be <i>happy</i> about that?”<br><br>♥ “Hmm … You’re wearing the f*ck-me look,” he drawled. <br><br>“And that would be because you’re so extremely f*ckable,” I shot back. “Waking up to you is like … presents on Christmas morning.” <br><br>His mouth curved. “For your convenience, I’m already unwrapped. Batteries not required.”<br><br>♦ "Sex radar. I has it."<br><br>♥ "Day One of my life was the day I met you."<br><br>♥ “You’re my lucky charm,” he said. <br><br>I squeezed his biceps. “Really?” <br><br>“Yep.” He licked the upper swell of my breast. “You’re magically delicious.” <br><br>“Oh my God!” I laughed. “Cheesy.”<br><br>♥ “Crossfire.” <br><br>My hands stilled on him. <br><br>He swallowed, his throat working. “It’s your word for when things get to be too much, when it’s too intense. It’s my word, too, because that’s how you make me feel. All the time.”<br><br>♥ “It’s starting to go away,” he murmured. <br><br>My smile faded. “What? What’s going away?” <br><br>“The … worry. It feels safe, doesn’t it?” He sipped his wine. “Settled. It’s a good feeling. I like it. A lot.”<br><br>♥ "I guess you like the ring."</span>
  <a data-text-id="15656445693639547821" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<b>"Just be with me" I whispered, my eyes stinging all over again. "I need you." Gideon's fingertips glided softly down my cheek. "You were with me, The whole time. There wasn't a second that passed when you weren't on my mind. You own me, Eva. Where</b></blockquote></span>

</a><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/david%20gandy/gideon6_zpsa4559e73.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379798593i/642931._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo gideon6_zpsa4559e73.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/women%20pics/c28b1d42-41e1-4fc3-9bc1-cd34666e5a2a_zps354165b6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>We start this love story where we are left after reflected in you. Eva learns what Gideon did to protect her, to keep her safe. They get back together but have secrets to keep so their relationship is kept quiet.<br><br><blockquote>
<b>"Just be with me" I whispered, my eyes stinging all over again. "I need you." Gideon's fingertips glided softly down my cheek. "You were with me, The whole time. There wasn't a second that passed when you weren't on my mind. You own me, Eva. Wherever I am, whatever I'm doing, I belong to you."</b><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/crossfire%20novels/entwinedquote2_zps04ad8aca.jpg.html" target="_blank" href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/crossfire%20novels/entwinedpic_zpscd02c1bd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380390642i/752464._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo entwinedpic_zpscd02c1bd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>There love seeps through the pages, this book has a very different feel to the other two books, I found it to be slower paced but I also feel that's what they need as a couple, to <b>re-connect, to heal, to come together, to be whole</b>.<br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/crossfire%20novels/entwined_zpsc04f2cee.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><blockquote><b>"I love you," he whispered. "Too much."</b></blockquote>
<br><br><blockquote><b>"Eva. Let me... "He cupped my face, licking deep into my mouth. "Let me love you."</b></blockquote>
<br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/crossfire%20novels/gideonandeva_zps13d5a440.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380390642i/752467.gif" alt=" photo gideonandeva_zps13d5a440.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><b>"Day one of my life was the day I met you."</b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/crossfire%20novels/gideoncross_zpseeb5c60d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380390642i/752468.jpg" alt=" photo gideoncross_zpseeb5c60d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I'll do anything for you. There are no limits in our bed. No memories Just us. You and me. And love. I love you so much."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Gideon is his domineering possessive self, he'll do anything to keep Eva safe and loved. They deal with lots of obstacles along the way but what I liked about them as a unit is they TALK about everything together, if they worry or are scared they talk it through. There is No stupidity or annoyance. I found them to be stronger and bound together. There scenes are intense, sensual and at times they fuck and times they are very much slow and love each other with care. they are very much <b>Entwined</b> <br><br>They are dealing with not only re-connecting but there hurt, there nightmares, there abuse. This is very much at the centre of there relationship and I suppose what drew them together, they are learning to deal with there pasts together.<br><br>They find there way back together.. and take time to come out to their world, their friends and family slowly, so so many great moments I have highlighted so many quotes I can't put them all on but go read it and love them too.<br><br>There's more Cary and his drama and Eva's love for her best friend, them continuing to deal with change and new challenges, also Eva's mum was there with her problems but even though she IS frustrating I enjoyed reading her too. Eva's dad adds his own moments with Eva. He loves Eva and wants her happy we see more of them.... also Gideon trying to regain his trust after all he is going to be Gideon's father in law <u>Eventually</u>!!!<br><br>This story is there next journey to there HEA but we have another two books to get through.<br>I do understand how people are upset about 1. the wait and 2. that they want them to get there HEA sooner, I am personally very happy I love this story and am happy to go through more with them, not just for Gideon but for Eva I can see how there is a lot more to come such as there nightmares, there torment, there family's, ex's. So if your worried about the length and thinking it's prolonging the journey just give it a chance before you dismiss this one!! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Eva." His features softened. "I can't change who I am, and I won't change who I am, and I don't want to change who you are. I just want us to be who we are-together."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>There is NO CLIFFHANGER just lots more questions to answer..<br><br>So enjoy and patiently awaiting book 4... <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/crossfire%20novels/entwinedgif_zps8424f289.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380390642ra/752469.gif" alt=" photo entwinedgif_zps8424f289.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I look at you, angel, and I want you so badly. I want to be with you, talk to you. I want to hear you laugh and hold you when you cry. I want to sit next to you, breathe the same air, share the same life. I want to wake up to you like this every day forever. I <i>want</i> you." "Gideon." I leaned forward and kissed him softly. "I want you, too."</b>
</blockquote></span>

<div id="review_427730240" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/427730240" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10149843-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593628440p2/10149843.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/427730240?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/10149843-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10149843-sarah?shelf=2013-releases">2013-releases</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer427730240" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6487284579882289645"><b>3.5 'disappointed but I'm gong to hang in there to see what happens next' stars</b><br/><br/>Ok so this is a tough book to review as it was originally a DNF for me. For all those huge Gideon fans out there.....let me explain.....<br/><br/>At the time of this first being released there was so much hype about this book and I was excited to read the FINAL instalment of Gideon and Eva's journey. I absolutely loved the first two books in this series, they were such engaging books and lets face it Gideon Cross is super hot, </span>
  <span id="freeText6487284579882289645" style="display:none"><b>3.5 'disappointed but I'm gong to hang in there to see what happens next' stars</b><br /><br />Ok so this is a tough book to review as it was originally a DNF for me. For all those huge Gideon fans out there.....let me explain.....<br /><br />At the time of this first being released there was so much hype about this book and I was excited to read the FINAL instalment of Gideon and Eva's journey. I absolutely loved the first two books in this series, they were such engaging books and lets face it Gideon Cross is super hot, who wouldn't love him? Therefore, like many I was eager to get answers and for the final pieces of the jigsaw slot into place........but just as I was about to start I bizarrely read that this wasn't the final book after all, that the author had decided to write TWO more???!!!........which to begin with surprised me but I assumed that the author had needed to write more books because there was just too much content to squeeze into this one final part, and so with this new knowledge on board I started this hotly anticipated <b>third book in the Crossfire series. </b><br /><br />Unfortunately within the first 15 % my enthusiasm dropped significantly and by 40% I made the decisions to give up. There was nothing majorly wrong about this book in fact the sex scenes were AMAZING, and no one can ever fault this author for the <b>fantastically erotic sex scenes </b>she writes.......but that was all it was, for 40% of this book, it was sex scene, after sex scene, with no actual story for me I'm afraid.<br /><br />HOWEVER......Last week I decided to give it another go. I love Gideon and I still wanted to know what happened despite the initial seemingly slow story .....I thought maybe it might be different for me now that all the hype has died down, so I started back where I'd left it. <br /><br />So now i have finished and all in all I have to say that I definitely enjoyed it more this time around but for me it was definitely a "FILLER" more than a complete story. As a reader I still feel a bit annoyed really because everything that happens in this book could have been condensed down and the story still would have flowed. There just seemed to be so much "padding out" of the story and I really do feel like this book was just a slow build to set the scene for the next book.....which i know some would be happy with but for me, when i'm expecting a book to be the final part, and what I actually get is a book that has such a slow pace nothing much seems to happen, it is a disappointment. Don't get me wrong the book definitely got better as it went along and we did get to see a bit more drama. I also loved reading about how Eva and Gidoens relationship develops and there were a few surprises in store for me,<br /><br />I'm glad I went back to it because I now have a renewed sense of eagerness to read the next book, and I know Gideon will make it all worth it in the end, I suppose I just can't help but feel duped as a reader......it just feels to me that story is being strung out a bit too much.....ad for me sometimes LESS is MORE!!!! <br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6487284579882289645" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <i>Re-read with my funny ladies; Supreet, Flo & Eda ♥♥♥</i>

I'm a little abhorred that I rated this 5 stars previously (that says a lot about my book taste back then, damn you FSOG frenzy and my desperate fix of withdrawal). <br/><br/>So this is my attempt of an unconventional review because honestly, I'd like to write a letter to this author. <br/><br/><i>WARNING: Spoilers ahead for Book 3 if you haven't read. But then again...I'm pretty sure 90% of you have already rea</i></span>
  <span id="freeText7145970902315926905" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Re-read with my funny ladies; Supreet, Flo &amp; Eda ♥♥♥</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380996949ra/3741330.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well...that's a whole load of bullcrap in one book. I'm a little abhorred that I rated this 5 stars previously (that says a lot about my book taste back then, damn you FSOG frenzy and my desperate fix of withdrawal). <br><br>So this is my attempt of an unconventional review because honestly, I'd like to write a letter to this author. <br><br><i>WARNING: Spoilers ahead for Book 3 if you haven't read. But then again...I'm pretty sure 90% of you have already read it. So moving along.</i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415443863i/11789676.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Dear Sylvia Day,</i><br><br>I'm not sure why you would make any reader wait a year and a half for another book in this series or why for a matter of fact, that you would not let this series end already. If you'd think that us readers have a memory capacity of a size of a whale, I'm deeply questioning your motives of even bothering to continue writing this series. Heck I couldn't even remember what I ate for breakfast yesterday morning, let alone the last time you publish this book. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416056661i/11883263.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Honestly I read 3 pages in and I couldn't remember for the life of me who the frak is 90% of the people in this series except <b>Gideon and psychobitch Eva.</b> Also her <b>annoying bisexual roommate, Cary</b>. <br><br>And who the hell is Brett, Corrine, Deanna, Magadelene again? Of course after some head cracking and thanks to my wonderful lady Flo who tortured herself with Book 1 and 2 re-reads, this was what I conjured up and correct me if I'm wrong:<br><br><b>Brett</b>: Eva's ex who is now a lead singer in a band who's still overly fixated on Eva (cue the music video scene in which depicts their old love affair) and is still dying to stick in his dick in her. <br><br><b>Corrine</b>: Gideon's No.1 ex-fiance and ex-slut. Centerpiece of all drama llama. Has a husband now named Giroux who can't keep the leash on his wife. <br><br><b>Deanna</b>: Gideon's yet another ex-slut. Annoying reporter who threatens to reveal about Gideon's past. Yet another drama llama queen.<br><br><b>Magadelene</b>: Gideon's idk-what-number ex-slut because<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416055939ra/11883245.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>And can we talk about that book plot....oh wait.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416056560ra/11883260.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously, all I got was <b>SEX, SEX, DRAMA, FILLER, SEX, DRAMA, SEX, FILLER, SEX, BACKDOOR ACTION, BOOM SECRET MARRIAGE, SEX, SEX, ABRUPT ENDING.</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416056560ra/11883261.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Why Slyvia, WHY?!?! There was just so much filler, zero plot and it was an absolute snoozefest for me. I literally dozed off 3 times whenever I attempt to re-read this. You should have just left this series at Book 2 and stopped ruining a possibly good series. <br><br>Honestly, I'm not even sure what's left to read about because Book 2 was a whole bullocks of filler and so was this one. And Gideon apparently gets away with murder, these two are shagging in every place possible and Cary knocks up his girlfriend, WHICH I do not give an absolute frak about. Just tell me, what <i>exactly</i> do you possibly still have to write about that doesn't make me wanna bash my head in?<br><br>So the million dollar question is, <b>
  <i>will I still read your next book that's coming out next week?</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393822749ra/8769160.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><s>Because apparently I enjoy inflicting pain on myself.</s><br><br>I'm doing this in the name of Gideon, SO LORD HELP ME. <br><br>You may win this time, Sylvia but I can't say the same after Book 4 is out. <br><br><i>Yours sincerely,<br>An eager beaver who is still pissed for making everyone wait.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415443863i/11789676.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To my lovely ladies who will be BR-ing Book 4 with me,<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416058603ra/11883327.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But I know we'll still have shit tons of fun, possibly ranting the hell outta that book ;D</span>

I am soo disappointed. :/ <br>...the slowness n the non awesomeness of the plot is ruiined my good mood n reading appetite from the very begganing... ;( The only reason I sat through this whole book to the very end..is because i ve never left a book as a DNF. ..n I was NOT going to let this book be its first....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400844ra/777257.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I'll admit this book does have Erotica leading it's grene factor.         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer426206218" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1393755523425693419"><b>Final rating: 3.5/5 stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i> Buddy Read with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/429926733' rel='nofollow noopener'> Georgia</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/458359738' rel='nofollow noopener'> Debra </a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/522576651' rel='nofollow noopener'> Joana </a>,<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/563099665' rel='nofollow noopener'> Ash</a>!! Thank you girls ♥</i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i> <b> “I look at you, angel, and I want you so badly. I want to be with you, listen to you, talk to you. I want to hear you laugh and hold you when you cry. I want to sit next to you, breathe the same air, share the same life. I want to wake up to you like this every day forever. I want you.” </b></i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Gideon definitely owns my body, heart and soul!!!!!!</i>
</b> ♥ Ever since i have read first two books, i have bee</span>
  <span id="freeText1393755523425693419" style="display:none"><b>Final rating: 3.5/5 stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i> Buddy Read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/429926733" rel="nofollow noopener"> Georgia</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/458359738" rel="nofollow noopener"> Debra </a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/522576651" rel="nofollow noopener"> Joana </a>,<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/563099665" rel="nofollow noopener"> Ash</a>!! Thank you girls ♥</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i> <b> “I look at you, angel, and I want you so badly. I want to be with you, listen to you, talk to you. I want to hear you laugh and hold you when you cry. I want to sit next to you, breathe the same air, share the same life. I want to wake up to you like this every day forever. I want you.” </b></i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>
  <i>Gideon definitely owns my body, heart and soul!!!!!!</i>
</b> ♥ Ever since i have read first two books, i have been eager to read the third one. Mostly because <b>
  <i>i thought it was going to be last one</i>
</b>. But alas, it was not and <b>
  <i>it makes me sad</i>
</b>. Because this book and story had such a great potentional, and now it feels like it was made only to fill in the time before the last 20% of the book. <b>
  <i>What could have been awesome book was turned into not so awesome bridge book.</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Anyway, that doesn't mean i didn't like it, cause i did. </i>
</b>But, there is one thing i found quite irritating in this book: it felt <b>
  <i>repetitive.</i>
</b> It was just like Déjà vu.<br><br>But never mind that, <b>
  <i>i needed my own personal dose of Gideon, </i>
</b> and i must say that Sylvia didn't disappoint in that department. There were many extremely hot scenes and it was just - too hot! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379787675i/498524.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> made by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/8278010-joana" rel="nofollow noopener">Joana </a>(great idea) and me &lt;3</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “There wasn't a second that passed when you weren't on my mind. You own me, Eva. Wherever I am, whatever I'm doing, I belong to you.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>CHARACTERS</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Eva:</u>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393058i/756684._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved Eva in first two books. Well, a little less in the second book but lets just say even less now that i have read this one. She just didn't stop being frustrating. Not to mention she became even more irritating than before. I understand that she was broken as a child and that all this is affecting her: Gideon going to such lenghts to keep her safe, her mother stalking her again, her best friend going through crysis... And she doesn't know what to do. But, she didn't stop being completely clueless and she always makes wrong assumptions - usually reacting before confronting the person in question. And the worst thing was that she didn't say important things to the right people... until it was late. Some secrets are not meant to be kept from loved ones - no matter what they are.<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Gideon:</u>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393058i/756685.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> made by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/8278010-joana" rel="nofollow noopener">Joana </a>♥♥♥</i><br><br>Gideon is the main reason i am still reading this series. His love for Eva is unparalleled, and yet, she still doubts him sometimes and it makes me feel hurt. Because after all he had done to keep her safe and from harm, she still doubts his love. <br><br>And after all, Gideon won me over and over again with all of his smooth talking and hot adventures.He will always makes me swoon :P<br><br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Cary:</u>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Cary is having difficulties, he cannot decide what he is doing with his life... He is juggling between two relationships in the same time, and i can't help but vote for Trey because to me, Tatiana is just like third wheel in the whole story. What shocked me was the plot twist near the end (well, depends on your angle... <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ but i was really surprised to see that he is going to have a baby O_O  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>). And, that is going to make big complications in both his life, and lives of people around him.<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Everyone else:</u>
  </i>
</b><br><br>-Eva's mother is freaking me and Eva out.<br>-Brett - i still don't like you.<br>-Eva's father is so awesome :)<br>-Ireland was cute as always.<br>-and everyone else were just ok.<br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>OVERALL</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br>I think it's sad that this is going to be <b>
  <i>five-ology, because i don't think it suits this series.</i>
</b> What could have been awesome finale<b>
  <i> was prolonged without any need, </i>
</b>and this book felt like all those "<b>
  <i>bridge</i>
</b>" books in series (bridge books are usually second books in the trilogies).<b>
  <i> But, the good thing is, i will have opportunity to read more about Gideon (even Eva) and Cary, which makes me happy.</i>
</b><br><br>I think the<b>
  <i> good idea</i>
</b> would be that <b>
  <i>the other two books are from Gideon's point of view,</i>
</b> because i am getting tired of being stuck with Eva. I don't know how i will survive the last two books being in <i>her</i> head <i>again</i>.<br><br><b>BUT PLEASE, PLEASE SYLVIA DAY, PLEASE MAKE THE OTHER TWO BOOKS FROM GIDEON'S PERSPECTIVE!!!!!</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Over and out.</i>
</b><br>____________________________________________<br><br>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●<br>____________________________________________ <br><br><b>REVIEW(S) RELATED TO THIS BOOK:</b><br><br>◈ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/426206201" rel="nofollow noopener"> Bared to You (Crossfire, #1) </a> <br>◈ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/426206210" rel="nofollow noopener"> Reflected in You (Crossfire, #2) </a> <br>◈ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/426206218" rel="nofollow noopener"> Entwined with You (Crossfire, #3) </a> <br>◈ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/609657729" rel="nofollow noopener"> Captivated by You (Crossfire, #4) </a> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

Her mum is a minx and I think we will see plenty more of her!!<br/><br/>All that said, nothing will EVER spoil my book love for Gideon, he c</span>

He is perfect, adorable, intense, passionate, romantic and delicious. He loves his lady so deeply and passionately and is fiercely protective. It makes me dreamily happy and all warm inside!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406681ra/793757.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>If his delicious character stays true, which it is has so far, I will always love to read anything and everything with him in. //<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nR2YuHlek7A5+UlTQu/EZ9bfNO984nB8OaZ14ngtkBanO/FqwgBa2J7S/TK1Gs64AIDTJ7Jv/hti2DNTtW5ijA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3zuREAgVBx3J2AxbD83F6cW/DuV9b4CkSCBkBfCJyublHfjCs0vOdW7zuDr4OM82E+DpLbPiDsMTXiK0Pco4fA==')})
  }
//]]>
